Hibernate:

        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE as col_0_0_,
        simulator2_.TAG as col_1_0_,
        maintenanc1_.TYPE as col_2_0_,
        maintenanc1_.VENDOR as col_3_0_ 
    from
        MAINTAINED maintained0_ 
    inner join
        MAINTENANCE maintenanc1_ 
            on maintained0_.EVENTID=maintenanc1_.EVENTID 
    inner join
        SIMULATOR simulator2_ 
            on maintained0_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch3_ 
    where
        simulator2_.BRANCHID=branch3_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        ) 
    order by
        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC

            on stock0_.BRANCHID=branch2_.BRANCHID 
    where

            or branch2_.NAME=?
        ) 
        and (
            stock0_.AVAILABLEQ is not null
        ) 
        and stock0_.AVAILABLEQ<=? 
    order by
        stock0_.AVAILABLEQ ASC

        count(simulator0_.SIMID) as col_0_0_ 
    from
        SIMULATOR simulator0_ cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch1_ 
    where
        simulator0_.BRANCHID=branch1_.BRANCHID 
        and simulator0_.SIMSTATUS=? 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch1_.NAME=?
        )

        count(borrowing0_.BORROWID) as col_0_0_ 
    from
        BORROWING borrowing0_ cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch1_ 
    where
        borrowing0_.BRANCHID=branch1_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            borrowing0_.BORROWSTATUS in (
                ? , ?
            )
        ) 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch1_.NAME=?
        )
Hibernate:

        count(simulator0_.SIMID) as col_0_0_ 
    from
        SIMULATOR simulator0_ cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch1_ 
    where
        simulator0_.BRANCHID=branch1_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            simulator0_.NEXTCALDATE between ? and ?
        )

Hibernate: 
    select
        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE as col_0_0_,
        simulator2_.TAG as col_1_0_,
        maintenanc1_.TYPE as col_2_0_,
        maintenanc1_.VENDOR as col_3_0_ 
    from
        MAINTAINED maintained0_ 
    inner join
        MAINTENANCE maintenanc1_ 
            on maintained0_.EVENTID=maintenanc1_.EVENTID 
    inner join
        SIMULATOR simulator2_ 
            on maintained0_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch3_ 
    where
        simulator2_.BRANCHID=branch3_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        ) 
    order by
        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC
Hibernate: 
    select
        consumable1_.ITEMNAME as col_0_0_,
        branch2_.NAME as col_1_0_,
        stock0_.AVAILABLEQ as col_2_0_,
        stock0_.RESERVEDQ as col_3_0_ 
    from
        STOCK stock0_ 
    inner join
        CONSUMABLE consumable1_ 
            on stock0_.CONSID=consumable1_.CONSID 
    inner join
        BRANCH branch2_ 
            on stock0_.BRANCHID=branch2_.BRANCHID 
    where
        (
            ? is null 
            or branch2_.NAME=?
        ) 
        and (
            stock0_.AVAILABLEQ is not null
        ) 
        and stock0_.AVAILABLEQ<=? 
    order by
        stock0_.AVAILABLEQ ASC

Hibernate: 
    select
        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE as col_0_0_,
        simulator2_.TAG as col_1_0_,
        maintenanc1_.TYPE as col_2_0_,
        maintenanc1_.VENDOR as col_3_0_ 
    from
        MAINTAINED maintained0_ 
    inner join
        MAINTENANCE maintenanc1_ 
            on maintained0_.EVENTID=maintenanc1_.EVENTID 
    inner join
        SIMULATOR simulator2_ 
            on maintained0_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch3_ 
    where
        simulator2_.BRANCHID=branch3_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        ) 
    order by
        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC

    inner join
        BRANCH branch2_ 
            on stock0_.BRANCHID=branch2_.BRANCHID 
    where
        (
            ? is null 
            or branch2_.NAME=?
        ) 
        and (
            stock0_.AVAILABLEQ is not null
        ) 
        and stock0_.AVAILABLEQ<=? 
    order by
        stock0_.AVAILABLEQ ASC

        branch2_.BRANCHID as branchid1_3_2_,
        stock0_.CREATED_BY as created_7_10_0_,
        stock0_.CREATED_ON as created_2_10_0_,
        stock0_.UPDATED_BY as updated_8_10_0_,
        stock0_.UPDATED_ON as updated_3_10_0_,
        stock0_.AVAILABLEQ as availabl4_10_0_,
        stock0_.BRANCHID as branchid9_10_0_,
        stock0_.CONSID as consid10_10_0_,
        stock0_.LASTCOUNTDATE as lastcoun5_10_0_,
        stock0_.RESERVEDQ as reserved6_10_0_,
        consumable1_.ITEMNAME as itemname2_4_1_,
        consumable1_.MEASURE as measure3_4_1_,
        branch2_.LOCATION as location2_3_2_,
        branch2_.NAME as name3_3_2_ 
    from
        STOCK stock0_ 
    inner join
        CONSUMABLE consumable1_ 
            on stock0_.CONSID=consumable1_.CONSID

        BRANCH branch2_ 
            on stock0_.BRANCHID=branch2_.BRANCHID 
    order by
        consumable1_.ITEMNAME,
        branch2_.NAME

            on maintained0_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join

            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        )

        maintenanc1_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC

            on stock0_.BRANCHID=branch2_.BRANCHID

        )

        distinct maintenanc0_.EVENTID as eventid1_7_0_,
        maintained1_.EVENTID as eventid1_6_1_,
        maintained1_.SIMID as simid2_6_1_,
        maintenanc0_.CREATED_BY as created_9_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.CREATED_ON as created_2_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.UPDATED_BY as updated10_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.UPDATED_ON as updated_3_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTENDDATE as eventend4_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTNOTES as eventnot5_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTSTARTDATE as eventsta6_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.TYPE as type7_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.VENDOR as vendor8_7_0_,
        maintained1_.EVENTID as eventid1_6_0__,
        maintained1_.SIMID as simid2_6_0__ 
    from
        MAINTENANCE maintenanc0_ 
    inner join
        MAINTAINED maintained1_ 
            on maintenanc0_.EVENTID=maintained1_.EVENTID 
    inner join
        SIMULATOR simulator2_ 
            on maintained1_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch3_ 
    where
        simulator2_.BRANCHID=branch3_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        ) 
    order by
        maintenanc0_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTID DESC

        maintenanc0_.CREATED_BY as created_9_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.CREATED_ON as created_2_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.UPDATED_BY as updated10_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.UPDATED_ON as updated_3_7_0_,

        maintenanc0_.EVENTNOTES as eventnot5_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTSTARTDATE as eventsta6_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.TYPE as type7_7_0_,
        maintenanc0_.VENDOR as vendor8_7_0_,
        maintained1_.EVENTID as eventid1_6_0__,
        maintained1_.SIMID as simid2_6_0__ 
    from
        MAINTENANCE maintenanc0_ 
    inner join
        MAINTAINED maintained1_ 
            on maintenanc0_.EVENTID=maintained1_.EVENTID 
    inner join
        SIMULATOR simulator2_ 
            on maintained1_.SIMID=simulator2_.SIMID cross 
    join
        BRANCH branch3_ 
    where
        simulator2_.BRANCHID=branch3_.BRANCHID 
        and (
            ? is null 
            or branch3_.NAME=?
        ) 
    order by
        maintenanc0_.EVENTSTARTDATE DESC,
        maintenanc0_.EVENTID DESC
